***осмотреть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осмотреть.html>осмотре́ть</a> (2745)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smotrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осмотреть.html>осмотре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osmotrétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осматривать.html>осма́тривать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to examine, to survey, to inspect</li>
<li>to see, to see round, to look round</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осмотреться.html>осмотре́ться</a> (8276)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осмотреть.html>осмотре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osmotrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осмотреться.html>осмотре́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osmotrétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осматриваться.html>осма́триваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to look about, to look around</li>
<li>to look round, to get one's bearings, to see how the land lies</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осмотреть.html>осмотре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osmotrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***основа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:основа.html>осно́ва</a> (1553)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*osnova</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:основа.html>осно́ва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osnóva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:основа.html>осно́вы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:основа.html>осно́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:основа.html>осно́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>basis, foundation, base</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fundamentals, essential principles, ABC, basics, foundation</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">linguistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stem</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">textile</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> warp</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:основатель.html>основа́тель</a> (10403)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:основать.html>основа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osnovátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to found, establish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">er</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:основать.html>основа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osnovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:основательный.html>основа́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osnovátelʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)основа́тельнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)основа́тельней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>well-grounded, well-founded
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:основательный.html>основа́тельный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:довод.html>до́вод</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osnovátelʹnyj</b> dóvod</i> ― <span class="e-translation">well-grounded argument</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>solid, sound, thorough, substantial
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:основательный.html>основа́тельный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osnovátelʹnyj</b> čelovék</i> ― <span class="e-translation">solid man</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:основательный.html>основа́тельное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:изучение.html>изуче́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osnovátelʹnoje</b> izučénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">thorough study</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>stout, solid</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bulky</li></ol>

***основать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:основать.html>основа́ть</a> (4266)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Related to, and possibly derived from, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:основа.html>осно́ва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osnóva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (unless the latter is a deverbal). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">osnòvati</i> / <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">осно̀вати</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:основать.html>основа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osnovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">осно́вывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to found, to establish</li>
<li>to base upon, to build upon</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обосновать.html>обоснова́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obosnovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:основополагающий.html>основополагающий</a> (18207)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:основа.html>осно́ва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osnóva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">basis, foundation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полагать.html>полага́ющий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polagájuščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, present active participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полагать.html>полага́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polagátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to think, to consider</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:основополагающий.html>основополага́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osnovopolagájuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>basic, fundamental
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:основополагающий.html>основополага́ющие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:принцип.html>при́нципы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osnovopolagájuščije</b> príncipy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fundamental/basic principles; guidelines</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***основывавшийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:основываться.html>осно́вывавшийся</a> (11771)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:основываться.html>осно́вывавшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osnóvyvavšijsja</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:основываться.html>осно́вываться</a> (11771)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">осно́вывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osnóvyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:основываться.html>осно́вываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osnóvyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">основа́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be based <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">imperfect only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:основываться.html>осно́вываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> чём-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osnóvyvatʹsja</b> na čóm-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be base on something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to settle, to settle down, to stay
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переселенец.html>переселе́нцы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:основываться.html>осно́вываются</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:берег.html>берегу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:амур.html>аму́ра</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pereseléncy <b>osnóvyvajutsja</b> na beregú Amúra.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The immigrants are settling on the banks of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Amur_River" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Amur River">Amur River</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to arise, to form</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">осно́вывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osnóvyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:особенно.html>осо́бенно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osóbenno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>especially
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:особенно.html>осо́бенно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понравиться.html>понра́вилась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:музыка.html>му́зыка</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%A0%D0%B0%D1%85%D0%BC%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B2,_%D0%A1%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B3%D0%B5%D0%B9_%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D1%8C%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:ru:Рахманинов, Сергей Васильевич">рахма́нинова</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Osóbenno</b> mne ponrávilasʹ múzyka Raxmáninova.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I especially liked the music of Rachmaninoff.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:особенный.html>осо́бенный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osóbennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:особенность.html>осо́бенность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osóbennostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:особенность.html>осо́бенности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:особенность.html>осо́бенности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:особенность.html>осо́бенностей</a></b>)

***осознавать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осознавать.html>осознава́ть</a> (11611)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осознать.html>осозна́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osoznátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осознавать.html>осознава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osoznavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осознать.html>осозна́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to recognize, to fathom, to realize, to be aware
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1996</b>,  Андрей Юрьевич <a href = vnd.unilang:курок.html>Курко́в</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andrey_Kurkov" class="extiw" title="w:Andrey Kurkov">Andrey Yuryevich Kurkov</a>),  chapter 59, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>Смерть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посторонний.html>посторо́ннего</a></cite>  | <cite>Death and the Penguin</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">ви́ктор <a href = vnd.unilang:покачать.html>покача́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голово́й</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:горький.html>го́рько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:осознавать.html>осознава́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бессилие.html>бесси́лие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> незащищённость.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Víktor pokačál golovój. Górʹko býlo <b>osoznavátʹ</b> svojó bessílije, svojú nezaščiščónnostʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Viktor shook his head. It was bitter to <b>recognize</b> his own lack of strength, his own defencelessness.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
